          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;

          flex-direction: row;

          box-sizing: border-box;
          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }
        .container-outside {
          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }
        .container-no-issue {
          padding: 0.5em 16px;
          font-size: var(--chops-large-font-size);
        }
        .metadata-container {
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);

          border-right: var(--chops-normal-border);

          width: 24em;
          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;
          flex-shrink: 0;
          box-sizing: border-box;

        }
        .issue-header-container {
          z-index: 10;

          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;
        }

          min-width: 50%;
          max-width: 1000px;
          flex-grow: 1;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          min-height: 100%;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);

        mr-issue-metadata {
          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }
        mr-launch-overview {
          border-left: var(--chops-normal-border);

          }
          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

I can't get Clusterfuzz to repro this, though I think there's an issue with where the subresources are located. I'll work with the sheriffs to try to get that resolved. Hopefully, once the Clusterfuzz issue is sorted out, that will help with the FoundIn-X label as well as the minimization.



<span class="line"><!---->I can't get Clusterfuzz to repro this, though I think there's an issue with where the subresources are located. I'll work with the sheriffs to try to get that resolved. Hopefully, once the Clusterfuzz issue is sorted out, that will help with the FoundIn-X label as well as the minimization.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For future repros, I suggest teaching the fuzzer not to use absolute paths. It makes things a lot harder to move around, and no one should be running python as root :)



<span class="line"><!---->For future repros, I suggest teaching the fuzzer not to use absolute paths. It makes things a lot harder to move around, and no one should be running python as root :)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I've also attached repro with the paths fixed so they work with relative paths. The following Chrome command should be sufficient to repro (assuming http server running on port 8000):



<span class="line"><!---->I've also attached repro with the paths fixed so they work with relative paths. The following Chrome command should be sufficient to repro (assuming http server running on port 8000):<!----></span>



<br>





$ out/asan/chrome --js-flags='--expose-gc --allow-natives-syntax' --enable-blink-test-features --disable-extensions --use-gl=angle --use-angle=swiftshader --enable-logging=stderr

The "freed by" and "allocated by" stack traces seem random. The type of object allocated and freed is not related to the type of the used object after free. It seems that the address of |bg_layer| is random, which may indicate that reversed_paint_list [1] contains invalid pointers.



<span class="line"><!---->The "freed by" and "allocated by" stack traces seem random. The type of object allocated and freed is not related to the type of the used object after free. It seems that the address of |bg_layer| is random, which may indicate that reversed_paint_list [1] contains invalid pointers.<!----></span>

Security: JavaScript after 'await getComputedAccessibleNode' is executed in a paint worklet context


          

(was: AddressSanitizer: heap-use-after-free box_painter_base.cc:970 in blink::BoxPainterBase::PaintFillLayer)

          (was: AddressSanitizer: heap-use-after-free box_painter_base.cc:970 in blink::BoxPainterBase::PaintFillLayer)
          <br>
        <!---->

To reproduce:



<span class="line"><!---->To reproduce:<!----></span>



<br>





1. Download repro.zip in 



<span class="line"><!---->1. Download repro.zip in <!----></span>





#c6



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c6"><!---->#c6<!----></a>





 and unzip it



<span class="line"><!----> and unzip it<!----></span>



<br>





2. Run 'python -m http.server 8000' in the download directory



<span class="line"><!---->2. Run 'python -m http.server 8000' in the download directory<!----></span>



<br>





3. Build DCHECK+Release chrome, and run with --enable-blink-features=AccessibilityObjectModel 



<span class="line"><!---->3. Build DCHECK+Release chrome, and run with --enable-blink-features=AccessibilityObjectModel <!----></span>





http://127.0.0.1:8000/fuzzer-testcases/fuzz-00015.html



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://127.0.0.1:8000/fuzzer-testcases/fuzz-00015.html"><!---->http://127.0.0.1:8000/fuzzer-testcases/fuzz-00015.html<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





After some time, the renderer crashes at a DCHECK. Stack trace is in 



<span class="line"><!---->After some time, the renderer crashes at a DCHECK. Stack trace is in <!----></span>





#c13



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c13"><!---->#c13<!----></a>





. The situation found by the DCHECK failure will cause use-after-free in an asan build.



<span class="line"><!---->. The situation found by the DCHECK failure will cause use-after-free in an asan build.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The sequence of execution when before the DCHECK failure (or asan use-after-free/buffer-overflow): 



<span class="line"><!---->The sequence of execution when before the DCHECK failure (or asan use-after-free/buffer-overflow): <!----></span>



<br>





1. <body>'s onload event handler creates an image element. 



<span class="line"><!---->1. &lt;body&gt;'s onload event handler creates an image element. <!----></span>



<br>





2. The image's onload event fires, and the event handler calls a huge async function trigger1().



<span class="line"><!---->2. The image's onload event fires, and the event handler calls a huge async function trigger1().<!----></span>



<br>





3. After some document cycles, trigger1() reaches the following code and yields:



<span class="line"><!---->3. After some document cycles, trigger1() reaches the following code and yields:<!----></span>



<br>





     var v3189 = await v2086.getComputedAccessibleNode(v1848);



<span class="line"><!---->     var v3189 = await v2086.getComputedAccessibleNode(v1848);<!----></span>



<br>





4. In the next document cycle, an element with background:paint(paintlet1) paints its background.



<span class="line"><!---->4. In the next document cycle, an element with background:paint(paintlet1) paints its background.<!----></span>



<br>





5. The paint worklet class registered as paintlet1 is to be constructed. The code calls the JavaScript constructor of the paint worklet class.



<span class="line"><!---->5. The paint worklet class registered as paintlet1 is to be constructed. The code calls the JavaScript constructor of the paint worklet class.<!----></span>



<br>





6. The JavaScript code after 3 seems to execute in the paint worklet's context. The DCHECK fails before the constructor in #5 returns.



<span class="line"><!---->6. The JavaScript code after 3 seems to execute in the paint worklet's context. The DCHECK fails before the constructor in #5 returns.<!----></span>



<br>





7. (In a non-DCHECK build): The constructor in #5 returns, but during #6, the stack of the current thread is corrupted, and a reference variable in the stack points to an invalid address.



<span class="line"><!---->7. (In a non-DCHECK build): The constructor in #5 returns, but during #6, the stack of the current thread is corrupted, and a reference variable in the stack points to an invalid address.<!----></span>



<br>





8. (In a non-DCHECK asan build): Dereference of the reference variable in #7 causes use-after-free or buffer-overflow.



<span class="line"><!---->8. (In a non-DCHECK asan build): Dereference of the reference variable in #7 causes use-after-free or buffer-overflow.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





You can apply the patch 



<span class="line"><!---->You can apply the patch <!----></span>





https://paste.googleplex.com/5911055793389568



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://paste.googleplex.com/5911055793389568"><!---->https://paste.googleplex.com/5911055793389568<!----></a>





 locally, and add console.log before and after the line shown in #3 in fuzz-00015.html, to show the above execution sequence with more details.



<span class="line"><!----> locally, and add console.log before and after the line shown in #3 in fuzz-00015.html, to show the above execution sequence with more details.<!----></span>

Does this issue happen only on the main thread paint worklets? IIRC the paint worklets could run on non-main threads depending on the feature flag (OffMainThreadCSSPaint), and it seems like the flag is now enabled by default[1]. If we no longer support the main thread paint worklets, could we simply remove them instead of fixing the issue?

OffMainThreadCSSPaint is indeed fully stable and shipped, however, not all paint worklets can run off of the main thread. CSSPaintValue::GetImage[1] is where we make the decision, which is based on the inputs being used by the paint worklet. Specifically, PaintWorkletStylePropertyMap::BuildCrossThreadData will return null for paint worklet inputs which are not currently cloneable to the worklet thread (e.g. rich CSSOM types). Until we can support cloning all possible style inputs we can't require all paint worklets to run off the main thread.



<span class="line"><!---->OffMainThreadCSSPaint is indeed fully stable and shipped, however, not all paint worklets can run off of the main thread. CSSPaintValue::GetImage[1] is where we make the decision, which is based on the inputs being used by the paint worklet. Specifically, PaintWorkletStylePropertyMap::BuildCrossThreadData will return null for paint worklet inputs which are not currently cloneable to the worklet thread (e.g. rich CSSOM types). Until we can support cloning all possible style inputs we can't require all paint worklets to run off the main thread.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] 



<span class="line"><!---->[1] <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/core/css/css_paint_value.cc?q=CSSPaintValue::GetImage%20file:css_paint_value%5C.cc&ss=chromium%2Fchromium%2Fsrc



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/core/css/css_paint_value.cc?q=CSSPaintValue::GetImage%20file:css_paint_value%5C.cc&amp;ss=chromium%2Fchromium%2Fsrc"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:third_party/blink/renderer/core/css/css_paint_value.cc?q=CSSPaintValue::GetImage%20file:css_paint_value%5C.cc&amp;ss=chromium%2Fchromium%2Fsrc<!----></a>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }

          padding: 0;

          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }

          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
